2023-03-12 22:14:44.777 +05:30 [INF] Executed DbCommand (24ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']

IF EXISTS
    (SELECT *
     FROM [sys].[objects] o
     WHERE [o].[type] = 'U'
     AND [o].[is_ms_shipped] = 0
     AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT *
         FROM [sys].[extended_properties] AS [ep]
         WHERE [ep].[major_id] = [o].[object_id]
